< Text>
A basement posing as a bar. ¬†What does this place have.. almost nothing.

-Canned beers

-No premium liquors

-Fruity drinks concocted with low quality bottom of the barrel, no name liqours that equate to nothing more than a headache the next day.

Service was practically non-existent. ¬†I finally had to approach the bar myself and that's when the bartender tells me what you see is what you get. ¬†This place is an after thought. Dishes are micro sized and touted ‚Äúto share‚Äù. I guess this is true if you consider 1 bite sharing.

Drink prices were what you would expect for SF, but not commensurate for the low quality alcohol being poured.

The only single redeeming thing about the bar, it had a DJ spinning good music. ¬†The entertainment however did not make up for the food, the drinks (liquor selection) or the poor service.< /Text>

< Text>
Fantastic barbeque, definitely my go to for when I want authentic BBQ and not restaurant ribs or pulled pork. They have everything you could want and the prices are reasonable as well. I personally like Blake's Big BBQ Plate because you get some of everything. I also got The Beast today and it's also fantastic with three different kinds of meat on it. Those two things are more than enough to feed the whole family and have leftovers for tomorrow. The staff is also very welcoming and always friendly.</Text>

Bottom line, great food and service. Very pleasing atmosphere. The aroma of barbeque, along with high spirits made my first time here enjoyable. Parking doesn't seem bad, menu is very easy to understand. There was a female cashier who greeted/helped my group, and the owner's son was a big help as well- both friendly.

Loved the aesthetic of the place, very clean and plenty of room.
I ordered a Tasha's trio which includes: 3 sandwiches. One containing chicken, pulled pork, and the last brisket. I had a side of coleslaw. My friends got some meat and salad

They were all delicious sandwichs, but the one top the rest was that smokey, succulent brisket. That white bread with mouthwatering BBQ slathered on tender brisket?! You guys are killing it! üíØ  Next time I go, which surley I will, best believe I'm going to get that brisket. Thanks for the hard work.  üëçüèº

< review>
This an awesome place to experience great barbecue made by hard working salt of the earth people!  I am talking about real food, like fresh baked beans stewed with chunks of barbecued pork, not canned.  The Coleslaw was fresh, and I loved the celery seed seasoning to give it that extra fresh flavor.  And the barbecue...well, you'll have to experience the tender fall apart brisket and flavorful ribs.  Even their spicy barbecue sauce was good, with a nice kick, but not too much heat to scare off most timid diners.  The establishment was very clean and the service welcoming. One thing to note is that their diet soda selection was out of order on my visit.  Overall, a rare reasonably priced find, that I hope will continue to prosper in this out of the way industrial sector!</review>

<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
We never anticipated finding such delicious and reasonably priced food in the area. They're located in an industrial park but easily viewable from the street. If you're a BBQ lover, you're in for a treat. They offer a huge variety of food, and so far we've tried their tender, fall off the bone, ribs, pastrami, pulled pork, pork roast, homemade mac and cheese, baked beans, and their cookies. We have yet to be disappointed! They're in the mix an amazing staff that is friendly, helpful and makes you feel like family from your first visit, and you have yourself a winning location to dine at.

Something to keep in mind if visiting with a larger group is that you'll easily fit on the patio, but the inside is on the smaller side with only about 12 tables that are mostly 4-tops. So plan accordingly.< /Review>

< Review>
I'm a fan.  Not the 'greatest' per say but still some really kind grinds.
I went with a friend and she recommended that I try the "Beef Brisket Sandwich" (sliced brisket, BBQ sauce, red onion and a sliced pickle on a French roll). @  $7.80
Instead I decided to order the "Pork Loin Sandwich" (sliced pork, BBQ sauce, onion, a sliced pickle on a French roll).@  $7.80
We split the Blake's Rings and French Fries combo: @ $5

So the experience we had was that this place was pretty crowded.  There was this guy sporting the coolest handlebar mustache; which I haven't seen in a long time. He took our order. We sat outside and our order came out rather quickly. The food runner was way nice and friendly.  While we were approximately half way through our meal another food runner going table to table asking about our experience.
Environment wise: Pretty cool: Plenty of seating inside and on the patio. TV's were set to sports channels and staff was super friendly.
Food wise: The  "Pork Loin Sandwich" was way to dry and I had to add BBQ sauce to help try and wet it up. Might've came in to order this on the wrong day.
Thank goodness I gave half of my sandwich to my friend and she gave me half of hers.  Her sandwich was GREAT!  I should've listened to her : /
The Onion Rings and French Fries were good.  The Onions rings were better since the fries came out a bit on the dry side and had to try and salvage them by the savior known as "Ketchup"

So here it is in a nutshell: Try the "Beef Brisket Sandwich"<//Review>

Again, a little too much BBQ sauce for me, but my family loved this sandwich! The sweet, BBQ sauced smoky pork complemented the cool, creamy cole slaw.
